  max(next?: number) { return this.value('max', next) }
}

class OfferFilterSome extends Multiplexer<typeof defaults> {
  sellPrice() {
       if (this._price) return this._price;
       const price = new PriceRange()
       price.update = this.update.bind(this)
       price.data = priceRange => this.value('price', priceRange)

      return this._price = price
  }
}

TON Contests 01.07.2022 15:00:43
The Hack-a-TON is about to begin! üòé

The TON Foundation has just introduced a new technology ‚Äî TON Payments or Payment Channels. More information is in the article.

The Task

Come up with an idea of how to use Payment Channels in the most useful way and make a prototype in under 48 hours. Gaming, streaming, traffic, finance or any other field.

Presentations without a prototype will also be accepted, although having a prototype increases the chances of winning.

Evaluation Criteria

This Hack-a-TON is all about a great idea and its presentation.

There will be no stability or security testing. You can assume that the parts of the payment channel are not trying to deceive each other and not to implement an uncooperative closing of the channel. Only a positive scenario is enough.

Don‚Äôt forget to create a website that demonstrates your idea and have:

‚Äî 2-minutes video of your project (screencast is also suitable).

‚Äî presentation.

‚Äî functional prototype.

‚Äî open code repository (optional).

You can host the website on GitHub Pages.

Toolkit

Fortunately, you don‚Äôt need to be an expert in cryptography or smart contracts in order to work with TON Payments. You can use ready JavaScript SDK ‚Äî https://github.com/toncenter/tonweb.

An example of how to create and close a payment channel, as well as sign and verify transfers - https://github.com/toncenter/payment-channels-example.

You can use any kind of communication protocols ‚Äî Web-Sockets, REST HTTP or others.

Your prototypes must work in the TON test network ‚Äî https://ton.org/docs/#/testnet/

A bot for Hack-a-TON participants to get test coins ‚Äî @testgiver_ton_bot

We do not limit you in the toolset, you can use anything you want.

More helpful documentation

‚ö°Ô∏èTechnical description of payment channels: https://ton.org/docs/ton.pdf chapter 5

‚ö°Ô∏èSmart contracts: https://github.com/ton-blockchain/payment-channels

‚ö°Ô∏èWallet: https://wallet.ton.org?testnet=true

‚ö°Ô∏èExplorer: https://testnet.tonscan.org
